But some stations are on land near the water, on lighthouses, towers, platforms, etc. In some cases we provide a picture of the station. \r\n\r\nThe stations are indicated by diamonds on the map. Gray diamonds indicate stations that NOAA said were not producing data when we checked. They may be producing data now (sometimes stations break down and then get fixed).
